# This file is a list of EVERYTHING that can be bought within 25ly of LODHARY
# NOTE LODHARY MAY NOT HAVE A DEMAND FOR THESE ITEMS IN THE COMMODITIES MARKET
# This data is useful for a station's Bulletin Board Missions where you have to fetch
# specific commodities that the station may not trade in Commodities Market
# or if you have pirated items and need to know the best place locally to sell them
# It is based on data in the public TradeDangerous database.
# You should not rely on the prices or stock levels
# But you can be confident about the locations
# For each commodity, there is a list by buy price [cheapest first] and a list by distance [nearest first]
# 
# KEY
# Station  - self explanatory
# Cost     - The last known buy price
# Units    - The last known quantity
# DistLy   - Distance in Light Years from the LODHARY system
# Age/Days - The age of this station's price data relative to the time that this report was generated at 07/04/2017-13:02:39.59 [DD/MM/YYYY-UTC]
# StnLs    - Distance of the station from the system star in Ls. 0.01 ly = 100 KLs
# B/Mkt    - Is there a Black Market at the station?
# Pad      - Maximum Ship Size that can land. Lrg implies that this is a station, Med implies an Outpost
# Plt      - Whether or not the station is on the surface of a planet
